<span id="freeTextContainer12588435033287405812"><i>“The only rule that counted was to not get caught.” </i><br/><br/><b>Masterpiece alert.</b><br/><br/><b>Esta</b>, our main character, is funny, smart and has her priorities straight. <u>She's perfect omg.</u> She's a formidable pickpocket from our time and has some old magic, <u>she can manipulate</u> time and also travel through it with a magical stone. <u>Her mission is to steal an old book from 1902</u> and in order to do that she has to infiltrate Dolph's gang of thugs.<br/><br/><b>Our second protagonist is Harte</b>, a <u>magician from 1902</u> who used to be part of Dolp</span>
  <span id="freeText12588435033287405812" style="display:none"><i>“The only rule that counted was to not get caught.” </i><br /><br /><b>Masterpiece alert.</b><br /><br /><b>Esta</b>, our main character, is funny, smart and has her priorities straight. <u>She's perfect omg.</u> She's a formidable pickpocket from our time and has some old magic, <u>she can manipulate</u> time and also travel through it with a magical stone. <u>Her mission is to steal an old book from 1902</u> and in order to do that she has to infiltrate Dolph's gang of thugs.<br /><br /><b>Our second protagonist is Harte</b>, a <u>magician from 1902</u> who used to be part of Dolph's gang but who got out and built a new decent life for himself. Dolph wants to steal the book Esta's after and he wants Harte's connections and magic. Harte is amazing. <u>He's funny, flirty, badass, stubborn and his mother is his weakness</u>. I want to hug him, constantly.<br /><br />AND GODDAMN <b>ARE ESTA AND HARTE SHIPPABLE AF.</b> I NEED THEM TO BE TOGETHER. THE <u>ENEMIES TO LOVERS TROPE</u> IS MY WEAKNESS.<br /><br /><b>The rest of the crew is amazing, too!</b><br />There's <u>Dolph</u> who's an older version of Kaz Brekker.<br />There's <u>Viola</u>, an Italian assassin who doesn't need her hands to kill.<br />There's <u>Nibs</u>, Dolph's right hand.<br />There's <u>Jianyu</u>, who's Chinese and can manipulate light and make himself invisible.<br /><br /><b>The last 100 pages will give you at least 4 heart attacks</b> because it's basically one plot twist after another, all unguessable and painful af.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2869036375" />
    <a title="Olivia (Stories For Coffee)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23837960-olivia-stories-for-coffee"><img alt="Olivia (Stories For Coffee)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1560536881p2/23837960.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2869036375?book_show_action=true">Jul 21, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Olivia (Stories For Coffee)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Olivia (Stories For Coffee)" href="/user/show/23837960-olivia-stories-for-coffee">Olivia (Stories For Coffee)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook " href="/book/show/34228491-the-last-magician">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2869036375" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3232127756831442964">Not my favorite fantasy in the world. I couldn’t seem to get into it, and I wish the magic system was fleshed out more because it had me muddled for majority of the novel. I wish I loved it more because the synopsis was right up my alley, but the story itself wasn’t what I thought it would be. <br/><br/>(Side note: the audiobook narrator didn’t help as well. The way she narrated the story made it tedious to listen to, so for a decent chunk of the novel I zoned out) </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2051458914" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2051458914" />
    <a title="Ronda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5304380-ronda"><img alt="Ronda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596526299p2/5304380.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2051458914?book_show_action=true">Aug 13, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ronda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ronda" href="/user/show/5304380-ronda">Ronda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/35647409-the-last-magician">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2051458914" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2446184120909785659"><b>4.5 STARS</b> <i>The only reason this wasn't a 5 star and sitting on my favourite shelf was because of the ending... but it was still utterly amazing...</i><br/><br/>This book, from page 1, was <i>memorizing, magical</i> and definitely something that pulled me in, almost <i>magnetic</i> in nature. I loved it! However, that ending was a little disappointing.<br/><br/>I've never read any of <i>Lisa Maxwell's</i> books before and I have to say I was pleasantly surprised, the writing style was amazing, the world building intriguing and the characters</span>
  <span id="freeText2446184120909785659" style="display:none"><b>4.5 STARS</b> <i>The only reason this wasn't a 5 star and sitting on my favourite shelf was because of the ending... but it was still utterly amazing...</i><br /><br />This book, from page 1, was <i>memorizing, magical</i> and definitely something that pulled me in, almost <i>magnetic</i> in nature. I loved it! However, that ending was a little disappointing.<br /><br />I've never read any of <i>Lisa Maxwell's</i> books before and I have to say I was pleasantly surprised, the writing style was amazing, the world building intriguing and the characters were believable, I fell for this book from page 1!<br /><br />My only gripe is the ending, I love a book where it does leave something to the imagination but I felt this could have been portrayed more, given a bit more <i>oomph</i> and not as rushed as it suddenly felt...... or was that me just being disappointed because it had to end somewhere?<br /><br />The ingenious workings behind the scenes had me guessing throughout the book, when I wasn't guessing at how it was going to end, I was trying to <i>foresee</i> the future within the pages, an amazing imaginative storyline, one that I could rave about for weeks... regardless of my disappointment at that ending, I still loved it!!!!<br /><br />Highly recommended.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2446184120909785659" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1699661466" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1699661466" />
    <a title="nick (the infinite limits of love)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2993271-nick-the-infinite-limits-of-love"><img alt="nick (the infinite limits of love)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1606193187p2/2993271.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1699661466?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="nick (the infinite limits of love)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="nick (the infinite limits of love)" href="/user/show/2993271-nick-the-infinite-limits-of-love">nick (the infinite limits of love)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2993271-nick-the-infinite-limits-of-love?shelf=historical">historical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2993271-nick-the-infinite-limits-of-love?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2993271-nick-the-infinite-limits-of-love?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2993271-nick-the-infinite-limits-of-love?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1699661466" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer999616899333724035"><br/>The Last Magician was a book I was more than excited to read. It has a heist, magic and a historical setting, all elements that made it seem like a book I would love. Unfortunately, the book let me down. However, I don’t think that should stop anyone from picking this one up, because I really think a lot of my lack of enjoyment of the book had to do with my personal preferences when it comes to book lengths.<br/><br/>You see, The Last Magician is close to 500+ pages long, and while normally that would hav</span>
  <span id="freeText999616899333724035" style="display:none"><br />The Last Magician was a book I was more than excited to read. It has a heist, magic and a historical setting, all elements that made it seem like a book I would love. Unfortunately, the book let me down. However, I don’t think that should stop anyone from picking this one up, because I really think a lot of my lack of enjoyment of the book had to do with my personal preferences when it comes to book lengths.<br /><br />You see, The Last Magician is close to 500+ pages long, and while normally that would have taken me 2-3 days to read, I struggled through this one for about 6 days. I was reading about 2-3 hours daily, and every time I checked my progressed, I would get annoyed that I had only made it through 20%. Additionally, I just didn’t feel like the book warranted that many pages, because there’s a huge chunk in the middle when the story in The Last Magician remained stagnant. I feel like 200 pages or so could have been cut down from this book, and it would have made for a more intense, action-packed story. Instead, it just dragged and dragged with no end in sight. Boredom and distracted not what I expect to feel when I’m reading a book about a heist!<br /><br />The characters themselves were decent. They weren’t in any way memorable for me, mostly because there’s quite the cast here, and I tend to struggle with big casts. The main character, Esta, I liked. She was very brash, confident and sassy, which made for great characteristics in a heroine. Her potential love interest, Harte Darrigan, I was very skeptical about. He was a little too mysterious for my tastes, and I’m still not quite sure what his agenda was in the The Last Magician.<br /><br />Overall, I wasn’t bowled over by this book I was expecting to be. The world building was good and had great potential, I just didn’t feel like the execution worked for me. But like I said, give it a shot if you’re interested in reading it because I don’t think other readers will have the same issues with The Last Magician as I did. Be warned though, this is apparently not a standalone.</span>
  <a data-text-id="999616899333724035" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('tpbAA1uhJkC6ypKifZz3WO34LlocmHjZEL/NqDCKyyoGuVA7TYd79Xqvys8RjBjZFOginVUxA9Cjndq9Tk08rA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('m2/mc4AMg0lIXrzIFFhROJLC6D+B4GJRVwt0+/AgEQcrQHZLlire/Ig75KV4SL65a9Lk+MhJGVjkKWPujufmgQ==')})
  }
